### [254] [Leveraging Commit Size Context and Hyper Co-Change Graph Centralities for Defect Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01132)
*Amit Kumar,Ethari Hrishikesh,Sonali Agarwal*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种考虑提交规模的文件级缺陷预测方法，通过将传统的过程度量重新定义为提交规模感知的过程度量向量，并构建超共变图来捕捉高阶变更语义，从而提升缺陷预测性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的文件级缺陷预测模型主要依赖产品和过程度量。虽然过程度量能有效补充产品度量，但它们往往忽略了提交规模（每次提交中修改的文件数量），而提交规模与软件质量有很强的关联性。同时，依赖图中的网络中心性度量已被证明是有效的产品级指标，这启发了研究者重新思考如何更好地捕捉变更语义。

Method: 首先将传统的过程度量重新定义为提交规模感知的过程度量向量，将标量度量转换为100维的分布剖面，捕捉不同提交规模层级的变化分布。然后将变更历史建模为超共变图，其中超边自然地编码提交规模的语义。通过计算这些超图上的向量中心性来量化源文件的规模感知节点重要性。

Result: 在九个长期维护的Apache项目上使用五种流行分类器进行的实验表明，用提出的提交规模感知向量替换标量过程度量（与产品度量结合）能持续提升预测性能。这些发现证实了提交规模感知的过程度量和基于超图的向量中心性能够捕捉高阶变更语义。

Conclusion: 该方法能够产生更具区分性、更好校准且在统计上更优越的缺陷预测模型，为文件级缺陷预测提供了更有效的度量框架。

Abstract: File-level defect prediction models traditionally rely on product and process metrics. While process metrics effectively complement product metrics, they often overlook commit size the number of files changed per commit despite its strong association with software quality. Network centrality measures on dependency graphs have also proven to be valuable product level indicators. Motivated by this, we first redefine process metrics as commit size aware process metric vectors, transforming conventional scalar measures into 100 dimensional profiles that capture the distribution of changes across commit size strata. We then model change history as a hyper co change graph, where hyperedges naturally encode commit-size semantics. Vector centralities computed on these hypergraphs quantify size-aware node importance for source files. Experiments on nine long-lived Apache projects using five popular classifiers show that replacing scalar process metrics with the proposed commit size aware vectors, alongside product metrics, consistently improves predictive performance. These findings establish that commit size aware process metrics and hypergraph based vector centralities capture higher-order change semantics, leading to more discriminative, better calibrated, and statistically superior defect prediction models.

</details>


### [255] [SERSEM: Selective Entropy-Weighted Scoring for Membership Inference in Code Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01147)
*Kıvanç Kuzey Dikici,Serdar Kara,Semih Çağlar,Eray Tüzün,Sinem Sav*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: SERSEM是一种新颖的白盒成员推理攻击框架，通过抑制无信息的语法样板代码来增强记忆信号检测，在代码LLM的数据污染评估中优于现有基线方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着代码大语言模型越来越多地使用大规模、通常非许可许可的数据集，通过成员推理攻击评估数据污染变得至关重要。现有方法可能无法有效检测代码中的逐字记忆。

Method: SERSEM采用双信号方法：1) 通过静态AST分析、基于拼写检查的多语言逻辑检测和离线linting推导连续字符级权重掩码；2) 使用这些启发式权重来池化内部transformer激活并校准来自输出logits的token级Z分数。

Result: 在25,000个样本的平衡数据集上，SERSEM在StarCoder2-3B模型上达到0.7913的全局AUC-ROC，在StarCoder2-7B模型上达到0.7867，一致优于Loss、Min-K% Prob和PAC等基于概率的基线方法。

Conclusion: 专注于人类中心编码异常比序列级概率平均提供了更强大的逐字记忆指标，表明SERSEM能更有效地检测代码LLM中的数据污染。

Abstract: As Large Language Models (LLMs) for code increasingly utilize massive, often non-permissively licensed datasets, evaluating data contamination through Membership Inference Attacks (MIAs) has become critical. We propose SERSEM (Selective Entropy-Weighted Scoring for Membership Inference), a novel white-box attack framework that suppresses uninformative syntactical boilerplate to amplify specific memorization signals. SERSEM utilizes a dual-signal methodology: first, a continuous character-level weight mask is derived through static Abstract Syntax Tree (AST) analysis, spellchecking-based multilingual logic detection, and offline linting. Second, these heuristic weights are used to pool internal transformer activations and calibrate token-level Z-scores from the output logits. Evaluated on a 25,000-sample balanced dataset, SERSEM achieves a global AUC-ROC of 0.7913 on the StarCoder2-3B model and 0.7867 on the StarCoder2-7B model, consistently outperforming the implemented probability-based baselines Loss, Min-K% Prob, and PAC. Our findings demonstrate that focusing on human-centric coding anomalies provides a significantly more robust indicator of verbatim memorization than sequence-level probability averages.

</details>


### [256] [Automated Generation of High-Quality Bug Reports for Android Applications](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01148)
*Antu Saha,Atish Kumar Dipongkor,Sam Bennett,Kevin Moran,Andrian Marcus,Oscar Chaparro*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: BugScribe：利用LLM自动生成高质量移动应用缺陷报告的工具，通过提供GUI交互等应用上下文信息，自动生成清晰、详细、准确的观察行为、预期行为和复现步骤。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 移动应用中的缺陷通常是视觉可观察的，但用户、测试人员和开发者提交的缺陷报告经常存在模糊、不准确的问题，缺乏关键组件（观察行为、预期行为、复现步骤），导致开发者难以理解和复现缺陷，延迟修复时间。

Method: 提出BugScribe方法，向大型语言模型提供特定的应用相关信息（如GUI交互或缺陷出现的具体屏幕）作为关键上下文，自动生成清晰的缺陷报告组件。建立统一的评估框架，定义观察行为、预期行为和复现步骤的正确性和完整性维度。

Result: 使用26个Android应用的48个缺陷报告进行评估，BugScribe生成的组件质量高于原始报告，并优于最近的基于LLM的基线方法。能够生成更高质量、更准确的缺陷报告组件。

Conclusion: BugScribe可作为测试人员和开发者的实用助手，通过为不完整的缺陷报告添加可靠准确的观察行为、预期行为和复现步骤，简化缺陷解决流程，提高移动应用质量。

Abstract: Most defects in mobile applications are visually observable on the device screen. To track these defects, users, testers, and developers must manually submit bug reports, especially in the absence of crashes. However, these reports are frequently ambiguous or inaccurate, often omitting essential components such as the Observed Behavior (OB), Expected Behavior (EB), or Steps to Reproduce (S2Rs). Low-quality reports hinder developers' ability to understand and reproduce defects, delaying resolution and leading to incorrect or unresolvable fixes.
  In this paper, we posit that providing specific app-related information (e.g., GUI interactions or specific screens where bugs appear) to LLMs as key points of context can assist in automatically generating clear, detailed, and accurate OB, EB, and S2Rs. We built and evaluated a novel approach, BugScribe, that generates bug reports in this way. To support the evaluation, we introduce a unified quality framework that defines correctness and completeness dimensions for OB, EB, and S2Rs. Using 48 bug reports from 26 Android apps, we show that BugScribe produces higher-quality and more accurate components than the original reports and outperforms recent LLM-based baselines. We envision that BugScribe can serve as a practical assistant for testers and developers by enhancing incomplete bug reports with reliable and accurate OB, EB, and S2Rs, thereby streamlining bug resolution and improving mobile app quality.

</details>
